    window.addEventListener('load', function () {
        var link = document.createElement("link");
        link.rel = "stylesheet";
        link.href = "https://ws1.postescanada-canadapost.ca/css/addresscomplete-2.30.min.css?key=XP67-TU34-DZ98-EE18";
        document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(link);

        $.getScript("https://ws1.postescanada-canadapost.ca/js/addresscomplete-2.30.min.js?key=XP67-TU34-DZ98-EE18")
            .done(function( script, textStatus ) {
                        if (typeof $ === 'undefined') {
            if (typeof jQRSX === 'undefined') {
                $ = jQBRF;
            } else if (typeof jQBRF === 'undefined') {
                $ = jQRSX;
            }
        }
        (function ($) {
            var isLoadingModals = true;
            var modalQueue;

            if (typeof $ !== 'undefined') {

                var centralQualParams = {
                    gigabitPreFlow: '',
                    shopQualModal: true,
                    resPath: '/BRSeShop/qualification/central_shop_mobility',
                    returnUrl: window.location.href
                };

                $.ajax({
                    type: 'GET',
                    url: '/eShop/Qualification/HowtoBuyMobilityForTaar',
                    data: centralQualParams,
                    success: function (data) {
                        $('body').loadingIndicator('hide');
                        setTimeout(function () {
                            $('body').loadingIndicator('hide');
                        }, 5000);
                        $('#centralQual').html(data);
                        $('.rsx-modal-group-wrap').addClass('central-qual-modal');
                        BELL.rsx.utils.initWidgets(jQRSX("#centralQual .rsx-modal"));
                        isLoadingModals = false;
                        $(modalQueue).click();
                    },
                    error: function (xhr, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                        $('body').loadingIndicator('hide');
                        console.log("Cannot load");
                        isLoadingModals = false;
                    }
                });

                $(".qualPrdSet").on("click", function () {
                    $("#qualPrd").val($(this).data("product-name"));
                    $("#qualOffers").val($(this).data("offers"));
                    if ($(this).next().hasClass("internetPackagePromoCode")) {
                        $("#qualPromoCode").val($(this).next().val());
                    }
                });

                $("#centralQualButton").on("click", function () {
                    $("#qualPrd").val("");
                    $("#qualOffers").val("");
                });

                $('#centralQualButton, .qualPrdSet, .qual-force-fibe-availability').on('click', function (e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    var postQualFlag = typeof $(this).attr("data-post-qual") != undefined ? $(this).data('post-qual') : true;
                    if (!postQualFlag) {
                        if (isLoadingModals) {
                            $('body').loadingIndicator('show');
                            modalQueue = this;
                        }
                    }
                });

            } else {
                console.log('Cannot load script');
            }
        })($);

            });

    });
</script>

    jQuery(window).load(function () {
        $.ajax({
            url: '/ajax/RSXHome/getMobileAbandonCartProduct',
            dataType: "json",
            cache: false,
            success: function (data) {
              if (data != null && data["Name"] != null) {
                $("#payless-abandon-cart-item #product-name").text(data["Name"]);
                $("#payless-abandon-cart-item #product-type").text(data["NetworkType"]);
                $("#payless-abandon-cart-item #product-colour").text(data["Memory"] + ((data["Colour"] != null && data["Colour"].length > 0) ? " - " + data["Colour"] : ""));
                $("#payless-abandon-cart-item #product-image").attr('src', data["MainProductImageUrl"]).attr('alt', data["MainProductImageAltText"]);
                $(".payless-container ").addClass("payless-banner-active");
              }
            },
            error: function (e) {
                console.error(e);
          }
        });
    });

<!-- Omniture Device Filter Tracking -->
<script type="text/javascript">
    var s_oSLF = "";
    var omniVal = "";
    try {

        function deviceFilterTracking(s_oSLF) {
            if (typeof s_oTrackPage !== "undefined") {
                s_oTrackPage({
                    s_oPGS: "device_details_filters",
                    s_oSLF: s_oSLF
                });
            }
        }

        jQuery(document).ready(function () {
            jQuery('input:checkbox[class=js-filter-selector]').change(function () {
                if (jQuery(this).is(":checked")) {
                    // differentiate blackberry and apple manufacturer and os
                    if (jQuery(this).attr('data-categorytype') == "OperatingSystem"
                    && (jQuery(this).attr('value') == "BlackBerry" || jQuery(this).attr('value') === "Apple")) {
                        if (jQuery(this).attr('value') === "BlackBerry") {
                            omniVal = "blackberos";
                        }
                        else {
                            omniVal = "appleios";
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        omniVal = jQuery(this).attr('value');
                    }

                    if (omniVal != null) {
                        omniVal = omniVal.replace(" ", "");
                        omniVal = omniVal.replace(",", "");
                        omniVal = omniVal.substring(0, 10).toLowerCase();
                        s_oSLF = "desktop:" + omniVal;
                        deviceFilterTracking(s_oSLF);
                    }
                }
            });

            // Product List filter omniture tagging which is not used in SPA version for now.
            jQuery('input:checkbox[class=js-price-filter-selector]').change(function () {
                if (jQuery(this).is(":checked")) {
                    var desktopId = jQuery(this).parents('div.rsx-listing-devices-filters').attr('id');
                    if (desktopId == "rsx-listing-devices-filters") {
                        omniVal = jQuery(this).attr('aria-label');
                        if (omniVal != null) {
                            omniVal = omniVal.replace(" ", "");
                            omniVal = omniVal.replace("$", "");
                            s_oSLF = "desktop:Pricing-" + omniVal;
                            deviceFilterTracking(s_oSLF);
                        }
                    }
                }
            });

            jQuery("#rsx-listing-devices-filters-select").change(function () {
                s_oSLF = "Dropdown:" + this.value;
                deviceFilterTracking(s_oSLF);
            });

            omniVal = "";
        });
    }
    catch (err) {

    }


</script>

                </div>
            </div>

<script>
    jQuery(function() {
        jQuery('#demo-loader-js').fadeOut('slow');

        var filter = getParameterByName("filter");
        if (filter != "undefined") {
            jQuery('.rsx-product-list-wrap-outer').hide();
            jQuery('.rsx-no-products').hide();
            jQuery("#demo-loader-js").show();
        }
        function getParameterByName(name) {
            var url = window.location.href;
            name = name.replace(/[\[\]]/g, "\\$&");
            var regex = new RegExp("[?&]" + name + "(=([^&#]*)|&|#|$)"),
                results = regex.exec(url);
            if (!results) return null;
            if (!results[2]) return '';
            return decodeURIComponent(results[2].replace(/\+/g, " "));
        }
    });
</script>
